Mr. Moon Sun-myung's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Realizing Heaven through the Official Path
<Prayer> Beloved Father! We have now entered the first moment of the new year, 1978. As we leave behind the tumultuous year of 1977 and welcome the new year, may Your glory, honor, mercy, and love be abundantly filled over all creation. Reflecting once again on the heart of the Father who has gone through many twists and turns in the providence of salvation, holding the grief of restoration, I earnestly wish for this solemn time as we greet the new year of 1978, recalling the historical heart that has been filled with sorrow. Although the past was sad, I think of the tremendous path of suffering that remains, as the Father, who looks upon the global situation in this present age, must continue the history of struggle regarding the tasks of fulfilling responsibility and restoring humanity. I sincerely hope and desire that this small group of unification, who are struggling to bear the grief of restoration, even through tears and death, may become a source of comfort that allows the Father to endure the historical sorrow. 

The Unification Church, which started in Korea, has worked hard until it has reached this land of America, having passed through Japan. When I think of the path of tears that the Father has endured, I once again express my gratitude before the Father. 

January 1, 1978 (Sunday) 0:00, Manhattan Center (New York, USA).
* This message was delivered as the New Year’s address for 1978 and is also published in <Words> No. 203. 

I thank You, Father. In the midst of the history of suffering, there are those who have betrayed the Father out of weariness, and through that process, You have comforted Yourself while looking forward to a day of hope, still gathering and relying on these struggling people as a target of hope. I feel once again how pitiful and miserable the Father is. 

Father, there are countless millions who call upon Your name on this earth, longing for Your children and the day of Your glory, but there is no one who says they will inherit the tears of Your heart, who will overcome the path of unjust suffering and bloody death on the battlefield. However, the group of unification gathered here today earnestly hopes to inherit Your path of suffering and the tearful path of this present age, so I wish for the Father to be able to release all burdens and entrust them to us. 

Having come to the center of this world, New York, after passing through Asia from Korea, we are raising the banner of struggle, becoming the target of attacks from all over the world. As we think of the Father who is working hard ahead of us, let us not forget that we, who have fought through 1977, have a historical mission to continue a more intense struggle in 1978. 

Father, may Your life-giving power be with all those who are praying at this time, welcoming the new year and new day. May the gifts of resurrection and love be abundant, and may You bless them a thousandfold, ten thousandfold, and protect them with the gifts of comfort and happiness, I earnestly hope and desire. 

Father, now that we have welcomed the new year, new month, and new day, may You, who have protected and been with us until now, allow us to advance vigorously into 1978. I earnestly hope and desire that the noble figures who vowed before the Father to achieve our goals by the middle of 1979 will be able to bring shining achievements and accomplishments before the Father, allowing us to be sons and daughters whom You cannot help but love. 

May we not be ashamed before the remaining days, and may we not become a group that causes heavenly sorrow by failing to fulfill our responsibilities on the path of restoration. I earnestly hope and desire that we may be strong and courageous soldiers of heaven who can fight day and night. 

Father, may the 365 days from this new day and new morning be days that can praise You in remembrance, and may we become a holy group that can fulfill our filial duty and loyalty before You. 

Father, please have compassion on the scattered groups in 127 countries around the world, who bear the banner of unification and the name of unification. I know that there are Your children working underground, looking for the light of life even under communist rule, so please be with them. Even if one life clings to You and cries out, may You become the joy, the flag of hope, and the glorious foundation that can surpass the world of Satan that boasts of millions. 

Father, may we be able to achieve this year's goals without fail, whether day or night, and allow us to raise the name of the Unification Church high in the world, shining together with Your glorious name. I earnestly hope and desire that we may become sons and daughters who have gone through the path of indemnity and are worthy of receiving Your love. 

Please remember once again Your poor children in Korea. As the North and South are divided and struggling in a sorrowful place, searching for a way to remain before humanity, please remember the poor Korean people who are striving to avoid being trampled under the claws of the communist world, and mobilize all spirits in the spirit world to protect them firmly. Thus, may they remain as the final stronghold of heaven in Asia, raising the banner of glory high so that all people may bow their heads and recognize and praise that there is heaven. I hope and pray for this on this first morning of the new year, Father, please remember. 

Also, please remember the group of unification that is being pursued and oppressed in Japan. May You be with them in their struggles. Father, who has personally cooperated in every tearful battlefield, please remember those who are pioneering the difficult path that others cannot. I earnestly hope and desire that Japan may be raised as the leader of Asia, fulfilling the responsibility of a sun nation that can represent Your holy name. 

Father, Your attention remains on the land of America, but I know that Your heart aches and is indignant at the fact that this land is tilting in a place of sorrow. Now, may all the white people unite and elevate You in this land, allowing Your original plan to save the world to be fulfilled, the original intention with which this country was founded. 

You have gathered many nations here to train them as a model for all humanity, to establish the heavenly kingdom on earth as a vanguard of Your holy will. Please mobilize the young men and women of this country to become heavenly soldiers and a proud group that can build the heavenly nation without shame as the future generation. 

Father, please remember Your children gathered here. As Your sons and daughters, who are bowing their heads to welcome the new year without shame, bless them, and may this time be one where we vow that there will be no sorrow left before the Father this year. 

This son standing here must not drive them harshly. From this moment on, there remains the task of 1978, where we must put forth all our effort and energy to achieve the original standard of the Father’s desire in the ongoing fight for 365 days. Father, I earnestly hope and desire that You allow us to carry out this task. 

We must not become a shameful group before the coming days, nor should we appear as losers before those who look upon the name of unification. I earnestly hope and desire that You take charge and oversee us. We are not a group gathered according to anyone's circumstances, nor are we a group gathered in search of anyone's happiness. We are a group that has gathered to seek the circumstances of heaven, a group that has gathered for the liberation of God. 

May we clearly understand this and become a group that raises the banner of liberation, dedicating our lives as warriors for the establishment of the heavenly nation, and may we be a group that struggles to become loyal servants. (Praying while sobbing) 

Father, until 1976, You allowed us to avoid shame under Your shining protection. I hope that by the time we reach the 1980s, when the seven-year course ends, all families and growing children in the heavenly families will become blessed families that can establish Your authority and prestige without shame. 

Father, who knows our circumstances well, we are in a position where we cannot complain or tire because we know Your circumstances well. Let us not forget that the mission You have entrusted to us urges us every hour and every second, and may You guide us to offer all our sincerity and intellect as a sacrificial offering. 

May we fulfill Your holy promise before the remaining world, so that heaven and earth may give thanks through us, and may the day come soon when we can be called Your beloved children whom You cannot help but love and be proud of as Your kin. 

On this time of starting the new day and new morning of 1978, please be with us, Father. Now, if the group of unification is in a lonely place, may Your voice, which encouraged us when we were lonely, and Your direct protection be with them as well. Please protect all their circumstances. I earnestly ask and desire that they may become a group that can rejoice and give thanks with heaven, a group that can remain in the struggle. 

To the countless spirits in the spirit world, may we not be ashamed before them, and may we not forget the heavy responsibility that Jesus and the twelve disciples, along with countless saints, are hoping for in this era. 

I earnestly hope and desire that we may be a group that can liberate the nation and the world entrusted to us, and I humbly present all these words at the beginning of the new year in the name of the True Parents. Amen. 

<Words> (The members greet the Teacher with New Year’s greetings and cheer. Applause) May everyone receive many blessings in the new year. Please be seated. 

Everyone, at the beginning of the new year 1978, we have gathered here. Since we have welcomed a new year, we cannot help but set new goals. Our mission is to realize heaven on earth. That is our mission. 

Realizing heaven on earth is our mission
You all know how important it is to realize heaven. Last year, the slogan was ‘Realizing Heaven through Families,’ but this year, we will set the slogan as ‘The Official Path to Realizing Heaven.’ What does that mean? It means how we will realize heaven. How do we establish heaven? This becomes the immediate task from now on. 

In looking at a nation, for a nation to be formed, it must have sovereignty. There must be a people. There must be territory. From that perspective, when we consider the issue of realizing heaven on earth, who is the owner of heaven? Who is the sovereign? Surely, God is the sovereign. And who is the people? The people are all humankind. Then where is the territory? The earth itself. 

From that perspective, today, is God the sovereign on earth? Are God’s people living, and is the earth formed as God’s territory? No, it is not. When we look at it centered on God, globally, God is not at the center. In America, for instance, is God governing this country? No, He is not. The people of this country are not all people who have a direct relationship with God. This land is not God’s land. 

Now, putting aside the nation, even if we look at a small denomination within Christianity, is God the owner of that denomination? All churches claim that God is the center of their denomination, but is God truly the owner and the center as they claim? No, He is not. 

Where will heaven be realized?
Why is that? Even within Christianity, there are hundreds of denominations divided. They are all fighting among themselves. Can a place that fights like this become the body of God and His foundation? No, it cannot. From that perspective, there is no denomination where God can act freely. 

If God has an ideology to realize heaven on this earth, where will He go? The conclusion is that He must inevitably come to find at least one family. Then, if the parents become one with God directly, and the children centered on those parents become completely one with the parents, God becomes the one owner of that family, and that family becomes God’s family, and the possessions of that family become God’s possessions. Is there such a household? 

You all have parents and backgrounds from which you were born, but can you think of any family that has become God’s family? “No.” Then where will God go? God will go to find individuals, individuals. Centered on one person, He will try to be the owner, and centered on one person, He will try to love in place of His people, and centered on one person, He can only be God who can say that what that person has is His.
How is it? Can you all say, "Ah, surely what belongs to God is mine, and what is mine belongs to God. I have received God's love"? Can you say that? God remains unchanged and is centered on an eternal goal, working continuously for 24 hours, throughout the history of this world for thousands of years... Is God asleep? No, He is not asleep, nor does He rest; He continues to work until now and will work again tomorrow. Are you all like that too? Then what does the realization of heaven mean? Where do we establish heaven? If the kingdom of heaven has not been formed, how can it be formed? This is a critical issue. God can be present in a nation that He can love; this is true. God can be present in a church that He can love; that is also true. God can be present in a family that He can love; that is also true. God can be present in an individual whom He can love; that is also true. Such statements are correct. If there are individuals, families, churches, and nations that can be loved by God, then God can be present there.

God can be present where He is loved. If a nation loves God, He can be there. So, have you all become such individuals? "Yes." Just saying yes... Is the path of love a winding road, or is it a straight path, a direct route? "It is a direct route." Is love present in the east, west, north, and south? Have you thought about that? "No." It is the center of everything. Because it is the center, it can encompass everything.

So, what is God's love? What does it mean to love God? How do we do it? How do we love God? If you say, "Today is the first day of the lunar new year, and I came here for God at this first hour, so I love God," is that love? "No." Then how do we express love? You need to understand that. You were born of God, but how were you born of God? You were born through love. You need to know that without being born of God and becoming a part of God's lineage on this earth, you do not have the qualification to love God. You must be born as sons and daughters. How do your parents love you, and how do you love your parents? You all know that without needing an explanation. It just feels good. There is no need for an explanation.

What is the first issue? It is whether I have become a son or daughter born of God's bloodline. This is the problem. When I was born, what did I receive in the midst of God's love? I received life and was born. I was born with God's life. Then, I received the love that can love like God. After that, I was born to live in the place where God lives, to live like God.

So, for whom did I receive life, love, and the ability to live? For whom did I receive these things? Did I receive them for myself? "No." Then for whom? Ultimately, it is not for myself. God did not make me to be born for myself; I was born for a common purpose. Therefore, in the end, I was not born for myself but was born centered on love for God. That is the best statement. I was born to receive love and to give love. Do you understand? "Yes."

So, I was born not for myself but for God's love, for love. God created me for love, and I was born to fulfill God's love. No matter how powerful God is, He cannot love without a counterpart. You need to understand that.

So, what did the teacher pray deeply about? "What is the foundation of the universe?" That is the question. "What is the relationship and core of existence in this world?" The answer is simple. It is the relationship of true love centered on the parent-child relationship. The "parent-child relationship" is the answer. If there is God and humanity, what do we see as the most ideal? What is the fundamental issue? The ideal, the fundamental, and all principled issues are about establishing a relationship centered on God's love.

When we look at this, there is no foundation to realize heaven in the world, in society, in the church, in the family, or even within myself. How can we proceed? This is a critical issue. Where should we start? From myself, from the individual...

How can God's love dwell within me?

So, how can God's love dwell within me? It cannot just be, "I will love God!" You need to understand that. For God's love to dwell in me, what must happen? My complete, true conscience and true body must become one. Only then can love manifest, and love can dwell. Why must it be a true conscience and a true body? You need to understand that. The true does not change. It does not go up and down.

Does your heart waver? Does it change, or does it not change? Your heart must not change. Whether it is difficult or easy, whether it is bad or good, it must not change. Just as pure gold shines when placed on a good pedestal, does it not shine when placed in a sewer? "No." Does it get eroded there? "No." (The recording briefly cuts out.)

What about the body? The body changes more easily than the heart. Is that right? "Yes." Then when can God's love dwell in my body? Look. If God's love is the body, and if the human body and mind are the legs, can the body stand if these legs are crippled? When love is the body and the human body and mind are the legs, if the legs are crippled and everything changes, how can the body stand normally? Can love dwell there? "No."

Therefore, how can we find an unchanging heart towards individuals, families, nations, the world, and heaven and earth? This is a critically important issue for fallen humanity. That is why we need a philosophy. There must be a way that says, "This is how life goes, this is how individuals go, this is how families go, this is how churches go, this is how nations go, this is how the world goes, and this is how heaven and earth go."

When we unite in love, equal value is bestowed.

Now, when I say that God's love has come upon my heart, will that love change when I go to my family? "No." Of course, God's heart does not change, but God's love also does not change. Ultimately, even if I enter the kingdom of heaven to love God, love does not change. The love of God in my heart and the love of God in the kingdom of heaven are not different. Wherever God's love is, there is always unity. It is unity. Without God's love, there can be no absolute unity.

When you enter heaven, whom will you think of as your center? Will you think of God as your center, or will you think of yourselves as your center? "God." But when you think of something other than God? Will that thought become God's thought or your thought? "God's thought." Then will God live with you? Do you want to live with Him? Do you like living with Him? "Yes." Is that good? "Yes." Is it better for God to always be above and for me to be below, or is it better for God to go below and for me to go above, to be round and circular? Which is better? The first option or the second option? The first option? "No, the second option." Right, I also prefer the second option. (Cheers. Applause.)

Now, look at the earth. Wouldn't it be wonderful if there were only night or only day? "It wouldn't be wonderful." (Laughter) It is the same principle. Your hair is you, isn't it? "It is us." If you pull one strand of hair, does it say, "Hey, why are you pulling me?" It says, "Don't pull my hair." It says, "Don't pull me." Isn't that right? (Laughter) Is your hair you? "Yes."

So, if you pull one out and think, "This is me," does it feel good or bad? "Bad." Why does it feel bad? Because it has already separated from me; it is not one with me. Why do you touch your hair when looking in the mirror? It is because you are one with it. Since you are one, you are governed by your love realm and can be united and can be in a place where you can receive love. When you are in a place where you can receive love and can unite centered on love, you are bestowed with the glory of having equal value under that love.

Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." 

Do you have a heart? "Yes." Where is your heart? You need to know that. When we say, "Where is the heart?" it can be said that the heart is where God's life is present. It can also be said that my heart can be where God's love is. My heart is where I can live centered on God. Why? Because God is such a being. That heart can be anywhere. Your heart is in your body, wherever it may be. Wherever there is love, wherever God's life dwells, and wherever God can live, my heart is there.

The heart moves to where there is more true love, life, and environment.

So, is that so or not? Do you all have a hometown? "Yes." Does your heart go to the hometown you loved in the past? "Yes." Does your heart go to your mother and father? "Yes." Why is that? It is because life is connected. The land of that hometown is connected to the living environment.

However, when a person whom you love more appears, you leave that place and go to where the person you love more is. Therefore, your heart moves to a place where the life force is stronger, where love is stronger, and where the living environment is better. 

When you think about that, doesn't it feel sad? Why do you have to stop there and not move on?

That is why everyone seeks a place of higher love, a place of higher life, and a place of brighter living environments. Moving towards a place with higher, more beautiful, and more true love, life, and true environment is the principle of the path of truth. Therefore, when you seek a higher path of love, you become happier. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

So, when the sons and daughters grow up and get married, do the parents put on the brakes and say not to go? No, they are happy. They do not say, "Let our sons and daughters not experience such love." Those who only knew their parents' love come to know the love of a husband or wife, and then they become parents themselves, able to love their children with a love that is at a higher level... Have you ever seen a father or mother say, "Honey! Why do you love our children more than me?" Have you seen that? Did you see it or not? "I have not seen it." Have you ever seen a husband abandon his wife when she says, "I like the child more than you"? "No." Did you see it or not? "I have not seen it." (Interpreter)

When you look at this, moving towards a place where you can receive a higher love, a more brilliant love is something that loving parents rejoice in, siblings rejoice in, the neighborhood rejoices in, and all beings in the universe welcome and rejoice in.

Why is that? Because through this, you become the foremost person who can gradually occupy and receive God's deep, multidimensional love, love that surrounds you. When God has sons and daughters who can love this world along with the universe, He becomes pleased, and when He laughs, the universe laughs along with Him.

When you give truly, consume truly, and love truly, a higher truth returns.

Does God ever say, "Oh, I am done being happy now"? Does He say, "Hurry up and be happy more"? "He says to be happier." When He is happy once, when He loves once and laughs, God's world becomes a world of laughter, a world of dance, and a world of song. Is that so or not? "It is so." Why is that? Because He is absolute, and because He is omniscient and omnipotent, once He is happy, He does not like to be sad. Do you like being sad? "No." That is right, isn't it? "Yes."

Why has that world not come to be, and why has it fallen apart, causing God to suffer and you to become like this? So, why did you come into the Unification Church? What did you come here for? What did you come here for, you guys? You came here to do fundraising. (Cheers. Applause) What else did you come here for? You came here to sell newspapers. (Applause) Did you come here for that? "No." 

Looking at your mindset, you think, "Today, even on the first day of the lunar new year, I have to go out and sell newspapers. While others are playing, we have to work." That is how your mindset is. Did you come here for that? "No." Why did you come here? You came here because you received true life from God, true love, and the ability to live truly, and you were born to share that true life, true love, and true living with others.

So how much do you share? Do you give 100% of yourself? Do you give 100% of your living environment to that person? That is the issue. Therefore, no matter how much you sell newspapers, this is the consumption of my life, the consumption of my love, and the consumption of my living, giving something true. You should think like this. If it is time, you share your time, and if it is love, you share all your environment. How wonderful is that?

What happens when you invest everything? Isn't that a loss in business? Does the teacher even acknowledge that you are doing that? He does not acknowledge it. (Laughter) When he says "Okay," does it feel good? (Laughter) Why is that "Okay"? You need to understand that.

When you give truly, consume truly, and love truly, that returns multiplied. When you invest your life, your love, and your living environment completely, and create a vacuum state, on that day, the more precious life of God, God's love, and God's living environment will come rushing in like a storm. That is the principle of the universe.

A true person is one whose heart and body are united. 

Because that guarantee is there, I do what I do whether anyone acknowledges it or not. Then, everything in the universe becomes a natural unity. Throw truth towards this universe. What will it become? Will it come as evil or will it come as truth, as something of a higher dimension? "It comes as truth." Why? How come? "Because it is the law of the universe." Why is the law of the universe like that? "Because God is like that."
So why does God do this? You need to understand that the universe can encompass both horizontally and vertically. When does the horizontal perfection, which we call human completeness, occur? The vertical perfection must come forth. When does the complete plus and minus happen? The complete plus is about seeking this. When the complete minus arises, the plus will stick even if told not to. 

In that sense, why did only women come into being, and why did men also come into existence? (Laughter) According to the laws of the universe, women are minus, and without a plus, a minus cannot exist. Therefore, if both do not exist, it cannot be, so men were created for both to exist. American women say, "In America, women are better than men," but no matter how much they say that, a woman is still a woman. (Laughter, applause) If you look at the body, women have larger hips and men have broader shoulders. When you take the subway in New York, when a man and a woman sit in the seats, it fits perfectly. (Laughter) That’s how it is. That’s the principle of the universe. Do you understand why men and women came into being? The existence of men and women is all a matter of heaven and earth. Do you understand? "Yes."

In the harmony of plus and minus, there is God's love, and God exists. When plus and minus become one, it exists eternally in God's love. Therefore, if there is only love, no matter how proud a woman is, even if she thinks she is better than a princess, she will say, "Oh, it's fine if you are better than me." So, everyone, is love good or bad? "It's good."

Then, are your bodies and minds united without changing? Are your bodies and minds one? Do you like each other, or do you fight? "We fight." You feel pain. Why do you feel pain? The universe can protect and nurture a being that is one with plus and minus, and it must exist that way, but since everything that is inappropriate in that realm of existence has become so, it drives them away. The power of the universe drives them away. Because it drives them away, pain comes. It hurts because it is pushed away by the universe.

Why does it hurt when you are sick? If you ask doctors, "Why does it hurt when you are sick?" they will say, "Well, it hurts because it hurts." Why does it hurt when you are sick? What does that mean? The universe is supposed to protect when plus and minus completely interact, but if it cannot interact, it is a failure, and the universe does not protect it and expels it. Because it is expelled, there is stimulation. When completely united, it feels good.

So what is your mind? Is your mind minus or plus? "Plus." So what does this plus do? This plus tries to make the minus relative. The body should naturally be one with the mind, but it cannot naturally become one because it is plus and repelling.

So here, there is a movement to make one minus. That must become the body. Strike the body. Therefore, religion has the purpose of creating a true person, so it tells you to strike the body, to sacrifice, to serve, and to do what you dislike. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The body dislikes all of that. The body must follow what it dislikes. The more you follow what the body dislikes, the faster you become a true person.

What the body dislikes the most is, "Oh, I need to wake up." (Laughter) But the mind says not to sleep, no matter how sleepy it is. When the body says, "Oh, I want to eat," the mind says to fast. Unification Church members fast for seven days. When the clock strikes twelve on the last day, you cannot say, "Oh, food!" At twelve o'clock, you must say, "God!" (Laughter) You must say, "In this opportunity, I will truly stand." Do you understand? "Yes." Then the mind becomes plus and the body becomes minus.

With God's love, the mind and body must become one for the individual heaven to unfold. 

So what should we do now? Adam and Eve fell in their adolescence. In adolescence, they want to go to strange places and want to go to the moon. They all want to relate to themselves. At that time, there is no one who is not a poet, and there is no one who is not a literary girl. At that time, if they become one in God's love, there is no one who can separate them. So if the mind and body become one and are completed, they can become true men and true women with true life, true love, and true living. 

So the feelings and happiness they felt in that position permeate their entire body and mind, and they think about that time throughout their lives, wanting to seek such places, wanting to live in such places, wanting to love in such places, and wanting to always place their lives in such places. They even think about it when they go to the bathroom. (Laughter) They think about it while working. (The recording cuts off for a moment.) 

God's love must be connected there. When will the body and mind become completely one? "When God's love comes." When you feel God's love, you cannot be separated from that love. You can look at the sky or look at the earth; it is just good. It is happiness. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

So where is your personal heaven? Where is your family heaven? "In the mind and body." Is that correct? "Yes." Because God exists, because God is present, and because God's love is present, that is the base of heaven, the base of heaven. Because God's love and God's life are within you, you can substitute God's life, you can substitute God's love, and you can substitute God's living. Do you understand? "Yes." Do you truly understand? "Yes."

How do my shoes look? The focus of these two eyes is seen from here, where they become one. If you look at the ears, all sound waves enter through the auditory nerves and connect. The representative sound is one. You have sound waves, right? Hitting one sound wave is the same as hitting another. When it strikes, the one next to it also strikes. (Laughter) That is where the ideal realization occurs. You must understand that the ideal harmony occurs there.

Therefore, when the body and mind resonate, they become one centered on love. This is logical, logical. Do you want to meet God? "Yes." You must have your body and mind united. It must be the same in speaking and acting to become a true person. A fake person has a different body and mind. They say one thing and act differently. Have you sworn a lot when your teacher said, "Let's do this"? But it was just words. (Laughter)

Can you achieve unity of body and mind with the naturalism and individualism you learned in America? Advancement and Leap  
Happy God’s Day to everybody! As you know, today is God’s Day. The time when God’s Day was established is today in 1968. So, in terms of cycles, it is the 11th time, and in terms of years, it is the tenth anniversary.  
God has not had a joyful day due to the fall of humanity.  
Today, all people on this earth have commemorative days. Among those commemorative days, there are sad days and joyful days. No individual or nation would want to have a sad commemorative day. On the other hand, it is human nature to want to commemorate and remember joyful and happy days.  
From this perspective, has there been a joyful day for God until now? Considering the fact that our human ancestors fell, we can see that God has faced a day of sorrow rather than a day of joy regarding humanity and the world. The day of the fall was the day God lost Adam and Eve, that is, His sons and daughters, and it was the day when God, in the position of a parent, became a miserable parent who lost His children.

Thus, Adam and Eve, born as the authoritative sons and daughters of God, as princes and princesses of the heavenly kingdom, fell to a position lower than that of a servant, to the position of the children of enemies. If humanity can reach the position of the parents of humanity, God may be able to rejoice, but without reaching that position, God cannot have a joyful day regarding humanity.  
The providence of salvation is for God to revive fallen humanity.  
Now, humanity living on this earth can be divided into men and women. Regardless of color, ethnicity, or cultural background, fundamentally, when we look at humanity centered on God, it comes down to men and women. The issue is how to bring these men and women together and present them as beings of the same value as Adam and Eve before the fall, which is the limit of God’s providence of salvation.  
Therefore, for all people living on this earth to return to God, they must go beyond the perfected Adam’s realm without falling. That is the fate they are bound to.  
From this perspective, when God looks at you, whether you are a man or a woman, one-on-one, can He feel a love greater than that of when He looked at Adam and Eve? That is the question. How about you? Today, the parents who gave birth to you love their children, saying, “Oh, how beautiful,” rubbing their cheeks and holding them.

**A New Morning of Glory**  
Good morning, everybody? (Applause) It seems good to hear such greetings on a glorious new morning, right? “Yes.” Everyone, it’s snowing, so it feels new, right? “Yes.” Seeing that, you will feel anew how great the power of nature is.  
Today, as you know, I will speak on the topic of ‘A New Morning of Glory.’  
Everyone hopes for a glorious moment, a glorious day.  
When we say ‘glory,’ can there be glory when one is alone? When we think about it, a glorious moment, a new glorious day is something everyone hopes for. The meaning of that word is to prosper. Then what follows is that light shines beautifully and abundantly. That light continuously and infinitely radiates.  
When we say ‘joy,’ individuals can rejoice, but when we say ‘glory,’ it has the meaning of joy bursting forth abundantly. When we say ‘happiness,’ happiness is not limited to one place but affects the whole.  
When we say ‘A New Morning of Glory,’ what comes to mind? It conjures up the image of bright light shining brightly. At the moment when the bright light of a new morning spreads, all things also rejoice brightly. The plants that were asleep in darkness all night, the new sprouts, all turn towards that morning light with a new direction. All the birds and creatures are filled with joy as they greet the bright light of that morning. How do you think the birds that spent a cold night in the snow feel when they see the morning sunlight? Cold as it may be, and even though it snowed, they will forget all that and welcome the bright new morning.  
What is a glorious day for America? It is the day a new country was born, the day when all the people of that country rejoiced and praised it. How about the patients lying in bed at that time? They will forget their illness and praise that moment. If there are people in prison, how will they feel? They will forget that they are in prison and celebrate that day. That time is a moment of joy for everyone, regardless of high or low, rich or poor. Don’t you think so?  
When is a glorious day for each of us? “Spiritual birthday.” (Laughter) Let’s set aside the spiritual birthday and say birthday; the day you were born is your glorious day. (Laughter) Have you thought about that? (Laughter) Why do they cry? If you say they cry because of overwhelming joy, that’s a wonderful interpretation. (Laughter)

Therefore, we need to quickly establish a church that does not fall into the existing churches of that region.

And if possible, buy churches that are being sold by existing churches. When the teacher thinks about it, if three churches are put up for sale in one city, they will be sold at a bargain price. They will be sold for less than a third of the value. On days when more than three come out... Then who would want to buy a church, who? To solve these problems, we need to evangelize, evangelize. We need to evangelize. If evangelism does not work, we need to pray all night and pray earnestly before God. We must pray earnestly.

Fulfill the mission of the tribal messiah and unite with the members
So when you go out to evangelize, you must all be spiritually guided and receive guidance; only then will it burst forth from there. Otherwise, there must be some spiritual force that allows people who are going to the market to come to your house. So how should you do that? You must evangelize with a heart greater than that of someone who loves you, with the same heart as someone who is searching for a loved one. If that atmosphere does not exist, it will not work. Therefore, we must establish external prestige. When it comes to "Reverend Moon," it cannot be just "What are they doing, what is that church?" That cannot be the case. "Ah, the teacher buys churches for all 50 states." That cannot be the case. You must buy them through your efforts, through your sweat and blood. You cannot do it without sweating and bleeding.

Next, fulfill the mission of the tribal messiah. This is a gift that God is now granting to all members of the Unification Church. Spiritual guidance is like that. A big tree has deep roots. That is a title. The relationship between roots and trees is the same. What does that mean? The spiritual world is the root, and today's substantial world is like the branches. Therefore, those who have many experiences in the spiritual world have deep roots. Do you have something emotionally flowing in that spiritual world? Is there depth? That is the question.

Therefore, when you make plans for tomorrow's tasks, you must pray about those plans and enter a stage where you can know, feel, and experience whether it is possible or not, and receive guidance. Therefore, you must put in sincere effort, sincere effort.

Next, you must be in harmony with the members. When we say members, until now, how have you thought? "Oh, that person is one who reports to the teacher..." and everyone has criticized, fearing they would be investigated. That cannot be the case. Those people can help you if you ask for what you want and need. They come to cooperate, not to cut your throat or cause you pain. Therefore, you must talk about your situation as it is. Those who are reluctant to have members will never cooperate spiritually. No matter how well they do, they will never develop. You must have a heart that welcomes members, waiting for them to come to your house, saying, "Oh, come quickly."

Look. Three years ago, when I sent missionaries from America, Japan, and Germany, I said, "When you become one in three years, you will develop; if you do not become one, you will not develop." It is difficult to become one. It is a difficult task, so we must do it; who else will do it? Think like that. We must do it; who else will do it? Therefore, I am doing it, I am doing it. Think that I will serve for the sake of two people and sacrifice for the sake of two people. That is what I am asking you to become. Then who will be the leader among those three people? Such a person will become the leader.

You must think that everything will naturally be revealed. No matter how skilled you are, if you scratch people, fight, and are always a problem child, always causing problems, you will never become a leader. The person who can always play a game for the sake of the three, for the sake of the whole, is the one who sacrifices and serves.

Will you unite with the members? "Yes." And will you unite with your family members? "Yes." It is not about saying, "Hey, you should unite with me." No, you must unite. Abel must save Cain to be Abel. You must understand that. If you cannot save Cain, you do not have the qualification to be Abel and cannot become Abel.

You all say, "Oh, the teacher sent me as the main leader, so listen to me!" What does it mean to listen to me? You must listen to those people. 

Become a leader who loves members with all your heart
It has been 20 years now. In 1957 and 1958, everyone... What kind of person was the teacher? Whether it was an old lady or anyone else, he listened to their words the best.
It was Teacher Jun. You need to know that. (laughs) He was referred to as the person who listened to others the best in the Republic of Korea. He played that game. Because of that, when grandmothers come, they try to share all their stories of love and inspiration from the day they got married. They want to pour out everything they have wanted to say until now. (laughs) Anyone who comes to see the teacher says, "The teacher listens to everything I say." That's the game they play, that game. After that, there is nothing left to say, so the teacher speaks.

308   The Key Player in Reviving America
If there is a vessel here, you have to turn it upside down and empty it out before you can put anything back in. When you listen to someone, you can't listen in such a fun way in the world, like that. You listen through the night, you listen through the night. Why is that? Because you are caught up in me. Am I being consumed, or are you being consumed? That's why in the past, people didn't understand the teacher. The headquarters staff said, "Oh my, the teacher listens to that grandmother all night long! Teacher, please drive her away!" 

You all have to do that first; they have to like you. They have to like you. They have to like you more than their own inspiration and more than their own sons. Only then can you say, "This is better than the world. This is more trustworthy than the world!" That's when work begins. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That's why it's one-on-one. You come to know all the secrets of that person. However, you don't talk about anyone else; you only know about it. It's the same for you all. You come here and listen to me... You truly listen to what I say, and you also truly speak what I say. That's the secret, the secret. That's how you exchange.

You listen earnestly, and when you speak, you speak with blood, sweat, and tears. That is, so to speak, scary. You all need to narrow it down like that. These days, when you give principle lectures, you are doing it ceremonially. You come as if you are going to work, keeping time, saying, "Let's have a lecture at this time." But that won't do, it won't do. That's why I issued a directive in Korea that when giving principle lectures, you should do it while sweating, while sweating. The long-established 36 families in Korea all do their lectures like that. They were educated that way.

When I preached in Korea, I was drenched in sweat all over my back. My dress shirt and undergarments were completely soaked, and sweat was dripping from my head. These days, since we use interpreters here, it's different, right? It's different because we use interpreters. It wasn't like that in Korea. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." That's why you should listen with sincerity and speak with sincerity. Is that how you are? You are to listen to one grandmother's words for twelve to twenty hours. You listen to them through the night. Since you have listened to everything, now it's time for you to listen to me. (laughter)

Otherwise, there is no secret to drawing Cain to my side... unless you stir up all of Satan's baggage and pour it out and get rid of it. You need to do personal guidance, personal guidance. Do you understand? It's personal guidance. Does a mother give birth to twins all at once? She gives birth one by one. Therefore, you need to sweat and put in effort, put in effort. "That person has reached a certain level. Therefore, even if it becomes one o'clock or two o'clock, if I talk for two hours, they will cross over." When that time comes, you should not hesitate to talk even if it becomes three or four o'clock. You must value one person's life. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You need to put in effort.

It's like a duelist having to point the tip of the sword first, or like someone aiming a gun. It's serious. You stand in a position like a doctor who decides whether someone lives or dies with one injection. You need to know how to treat life as precious. Do you all think about that? "Ah! The principle words," you just think without any thought. What is that? If you do it without taking responsibility, it's like taking a sword and stabbing. You are killing many people, many people.

Wherever you go, you must become a person who causes issues of goodwill.
That's why when you set up a person who has gone through the process, you must unite with Cain and his family. If an IOWC member comes and says, "Ah, I am the subject, so you must come to me and unite," that household will not come back. Their hearts are not drawn. If that person has traveled three, four, or five hours to come, you must respect that they have spent five hours.

Who are they coming for? They are coming for this earth, for this earth. Therefore, you must treat it as your own work, as your own work. If they have shared many words, you should be grateful for that and uplift that person.

310   The Key Player in Reviving America
Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You must not just be a person who can give orders. You must be a person who can receive orders and also give orders; only then will that person develop. I believe that a person who receives ten orders and says they will carry out three can become a saint. Such a person will be needed wherever they go. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

Then try to do that. Just giving orders and saying, "Do this," and "Do that," and sleeping during the day, you will be punished, punished. God will say, "You rascal!" That's what the teacher thinks. Such groups are all exploiters of life. They are all exploiters of life.

So, do you want to become one or not? "Yes, we do." So who will create oneness? "We will." It's you, you. What do you need to do to become one? You must continuously raise issues of goodwill. You must continuously raise issues of goodwill. You can create organizations in your neighborhood to promote speaking movements or singing movements. All of that is good. You can also hold good lectures and throw a 60th birthday party. You can do all of that. In every neighborhood, you can do a small-scale fundraising movement, visit homes with grandmothers, read newspapers, and provide commentary. That's what you are to do. You are to raise issues of goodwill. When you go out on the street, you should take young people with you and do good deeds in the neighborhood. Raise issues of goodwill. Raise issues.

Did the teacher raise issues or not? "He did." He gathered many people at Madison Square Garden and raised issues in New York. The same goes for the Yankee Stadium event. He raised issues. I went to Gloucester and raised issues while catching tunas. I went out early in the morning and raised issues. While others were having breakfast at eight o'clock, these guys went out early in the morning to catch them, which was unpleasant. I was always a person who raised issues for the sake of success and leaving something unique behind. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

While fighting with the reporters, I said, "Do you think you can get away with this?" You must know how to fight. You must not turn a blind eye when you see something. When it's time to fight, you must fight. At the very least, to restore the principle, you must know how to engage in a fight of goodwill. I am that kind of person. I have come to realize that God likes such things. God does not like those who are weak and get beaten while listening. God does not like those who are humble because they are powerless. You must bow your head with strength. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

I do not want you to do that. I like Tiger Park (the nickname of Park Jong-koo), and even while punching him, I like him. (laughs) That is necessary. Do you want to be humiliated and treated poorly? No, I do not want that. Since I am the leader of the Unification Church, I am like this; I do not lose. Why do I get insulted? Why do I get insulted on the street? Because I am the leader of the Unification Church. Sometimes, Reverend Moon often regrets becoming the founder of the Unification Church. "You rascal! You rascal! What is this!" Look. A person like the teacher, with small eyes, has no fear. A person with big eyes is often scared. (laughs) That's true.

In the world of goodwill, it is necessary to raise issues. Why? If there is a pastor opposing you, why can't you fight? You can verbally attack without throwing punches. You go and negotiate. There is no other way. There are many times when a fist is faster than words. That's how Satan is, that's how Satan is. When someone becomes weaker than them, they invade. They invade and hit. You must know that. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The teacher is a person with two sides. Think about whether you would play such games with me. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You must feel the thrill of presenting a big issue and looking at it pleasantly. I am trying to do that even in the U.S. Congress, and it has all gone according to my thoughts. I have explained everything about the Unification Church to the U.S. Department of State and other departments. Do you understand what I mean, you guys? "Yes."

The person in charge must have the courage to do anything.
312   The Key Player in Reviving America
You, the person in charge of Alaska, right? In a small place like Anchorage, I would turn it upside down within a week. I was a person who would stay up all night knowing where the nests are and what is where within a five-mile radius of the neighborhood. Only after knowing that would I go to sleep. If my father or mother needed wood, I would immediately go and cut it down. I had already seen where it was beforehand. I would go and cut enough to use right away. That's how it should be. You must dig and dig and select the best.

If there is a nail, you catch any fish around it. If you can't catch it, you set up a motor pump and drain it for 24 hours, a week, all night long. I am a person who has spent 40 days working hard to catch one fish, keeping the light on at night, sharing meals, and working day and night. You must take responsibility for a week with that kind of courage; otherwise, will you pack your bags and leave?

Before I succeeded in America, I decided not to leave until I succeeded. Now I have succeeded. Do you understand? You must raise issues of goodwill. I often feel sorry for this. If I don't have $50,000 or $300,000, why can't I use means to evangelize rich ladies? I feel sorry for that. You can evangelize rich ladies. Why can't you do it when you look so charming? You can earn dozens of times that amount. That's right, that's right.

Think about what kind of history the teacher has made. When things get urgent, I mobilize from the spirit world and say, "How much money does so-and-so need right now? If you go to such-and-such place and sell such-and-such, you will get this much. Bring it to them!" That has happened countless times, countless times. Once I tied my towel and made up my mind, I did everything without stealing.

That's how people are. A man must know how to farm and also how to play. That is necessary. If a lady is walking by, you kick her and say, "Oh, I'm sorry." Then you become friends with everyone. (laughs) Then that lady will say, "I've never seen someone so humble and so apologetic." That's how you become friends. You can make friends like that.

I can joke better than anyone else. I can say, "Why are you wearing your tie like that?" and tease them. You must know how to do that. Even if you are a great person, that is necessary. And you can say, "What do you have in your wallet? Do you smoke?" and check what kind of cigarettes they smoke. Then you laugh. When men do that, they become friends. Because of that wallet, you can turn a ten-year friendship into a friendship in a day or a few hours.

At that time, you can go and buy them lunch and say, "You look like my younger brother, you look like my uncle." You can lead them all like that. Why can't you make friends with people? You know, Dr. Dust's wife, who is she? Mrs. Duster. I like that wife because wherever she goes, she makes friends. Men like her too, and she immediately connects with them. That's why she is good at evangelizing. That is necessary. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." So, you must raise issues of goodwill.

Why do you need to do such things? To save the world... Is the world small? It's big, right? Therefore, you must raise big issues of goodwill. Then, what about the democratic world and our mission? We have responsibilities entrusted to us. What comes next? Each state and each country needs propaganda. You must know how to do propaganda. When you do propaganda, if you say, "Wow, Reverend Moon is a really good person," that will be heard once and forgotten. But if you say, "Reverend Moon is an exploiter, Reverend Moon is a brainwasher, Reverend Moon is a bad person," that is good. That propaganda method is the best.

You must start with love and service in your local area.
To become famous, the governor of your area must see you as an enemy, and you must be able to do that to become famous. If you become like Hitler, what's wrong with that? If America loses, Hitler becomes a hero. At that time, is he a dictator? 
314   The Key Player in Reviving America
That's why if I say, "You are like Reverend Moon, who is like Hitler," I will say, "I am a person like Hitler. However, I will be a victorious Hitler, not a Hitler who loses to the American people." (laughs) Is that a bad thought? God would like such a person. I thought so.

Now, Reverend Moon has done global propaganda without spending money, right? When some big event happens in the world, it all passes in three days. In three days, it all passes. In three days, new news keeps coming up, so everything disappears. But what about the Reverend Moon incident? Has it passed? (laughs) Has it passed? Are you curious and lingering? You are curious. You are curious. If you think it's bad, it should all disappear, but everything remains. Now, if I show up somewhere, will many people gather or not? "They will." They will gather. That is the fastest way. Stand on the side of justice and gather. If that country gathers, you can become a hero for that country.

Now, what comes next is prayer and service. Who will you serve? Who will you serve? You must serve your own wife, your own mother, your own siblings more than serving others. You must know that. You are not to go out and serve; you must serve within your own home, within your own home. You must serve from small places. You must understand that. Until now, the concept of service has been, "Oh, the country." The country is far away.
What you should do is to your wife, to your children, and to your siblings. Therefore, if you want to serve, you should do it first for your family. First is family, then home, and society. So it's the opposite, the opposite. Family, home, society, nation, and the world go out in reverse order. Do you understand? Christians are like that, right? They fight at home and conspire to do bad things while saying, "Let's live for the country." That cannot be. That is the height of hypocrisy. For that reason, you must earn respect from your wife and your children. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." You should respect those who live close to you, those who share your blanket, like God.

You must become someone who thinks about what you will leave behind and prepares for it. What will you leave behind in 1978? You must always resolve this. What will you leave behind in 1978 and 1979? You should resolve this throughout your life. What will you leave behind today, this month, this year? It is a serious matter. So, you have been in the Unification Church for a few years now; what have you left behind? Now, when I think about coming to America, I ask, "What have you, Reverend Moon, accomplished in America?" I am seriously asking myself. What have I left behind with my name...? I resolve to leave certain things in the future. Do you think about that? Those who cannot leave anything behind in this land will be accused in the afterlife. There will be no place to stay anywhere. So you must resolve this at any time.

That is why, during lectures, I must think about what I will leave behind during the lecture time. When I speak, I must consider what I will leave behind through my words. When my hands move, I must think about what I will leave behind. When I take action, I must think about what I will leave behind. You must resolve all of this. Therefore, even while walking a difficult path, even while walking a tiring path, you must ponder what you will leave behind, what you will leave behind. You must keep that in mind. You cannot be tired. The more difficult it gets, the more you must immerse yourself in those thoughts. That is what is needed.

What will students leave behind during their student days? What will you leave behind during the pioneering era? You must resolve this in everything. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." In interpersonal relationships, what will you leave behind? You must completely think about that.

Do not forget that you will die once. You will definitely die once. I don't know if this makes you feel uncomfortable, but... Do you know when you might die? "Well, those who die have nothing to do with me; they will die, but I won't!" Is that so? Are you confident in that?

Think about how much time you have left before you die. What gift will you bring before God? What will you bring? If you haven't prepared that today, you should weep. What kind of gift should you prepare? Death is coming. Death is approaching. Therefore, you must be someone who can wait for death with gifts that can be taken to the heavenly kingdom. You must fulfill your responsibilities in 1978.

I believe that a true religious person is someone who fights with death in front of them. A true religious person is someone who believes and fights every day with death in front of them. Do you agree? Think about that. That is why I encourage you to visit cemeteries often, to the cemetery. Do not go in the morning when it is bright; go at night, under the moonlight. It is a very serious matter.

Next, we will enter the era of forming international task forces. Earlier, I said to evangelize quickly with more than 40 people, right? You need more than 40 people to deploy a task force. In the future, we will need the UK. If America opposes us, we must focus our efforts on the UK. As I mentioned earlier, I have this thought. Next, the Peace Professors Council and the Principle Research Association. You should create that quickly. That must be prepared in each country. What you do is the same. Including universities, media organizations, churches, schools, and leaders...

Then, you must join forces with leaders from all sectors. You must prepare this content this year and take a leading role in joining forces with local leaders. You must understand that this is the reality. If you do this, you will be praised wherever you go, and heaven will cooperate with you everywhere. You must evangelize at least one person a month and definitely give Principle lectures three times a day. Even if you don't want to, you must do it.

Now, let's wrap this up. What time is it? "It's 1:15." It's still morning. When should we hold the next meeting? Since today is February 13, shall we meet around the 13th of next month? "On Parents' Day..." That's too late. Let's do it in mid-March. Let's do it on March 15. Is that okay? "Yes." At that time, the members of the order do not need to come. I will specially invite them to come... Now, we plan to meet once every two or three months. Do you understand what I mean? March 15. *
